pointing at stale entrypoint paths until the user manually reruns `openclaw doctor --fix`. This PR teaches the install flow to reuse the existing gateway service repair logic during `postinstall`, so upgrades can refresh that stale LaunchAgent configuration automatically instead of silently breaking the gateway on the next restart.\\n\\nThe new repair path stays intentionally narrow. It only runs for global npm installs on Darwin, only when the default gateway LaunchAgent plist already exists, and it never fails the install if the repair cannot run. The postinstall shim loads a dedicated bundled entry, invokes the existing doctor-backed service repair in a non-interactive mode, and converts repair failures into warnings. Regression tests cover the positive repair path, the explicit opt-out env var, and the error-swallowing behavior.\\n\\n## Testing\\n\\n- `pnpm exec vitest run
